  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_7a095a56-7f10-4251-b3e0-aae4aaf4b91e'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();

      initializeSiwa();
    }

  <span id="freeText12504762102906850534" style="display:none"><b>From the USA Today Bestselling Sweet Home Series, comes Sweet Hope.</b><br /><br />My name is Ally Prince and I've always been unlucky in love. I don’t know why, I just always… have.<br /><br />When all of my best friends were falling for their soul mates in College, I was left behind. I was Ally, the pretty cousin of superstar quarterback, Romeo Prince. I was Ally, the best friend to the most amazing group of girls I've ever known—a title I loved, but one I became tired of 'just' being. And I was Ally, the one on which they could all rely.<br /><br />But to me, I was Ally, the girl with the heart no one had claimed... And I was, Ally, the girl, who underneath it all, was heart-breakingly lonely.<br /><br />I LOVE love; the thought of it, the nervous excitement of falling for Mr. Right, the desire of someone becoming my entire world... of me becoming theirs. I’ve always wanted passion, heart-stopping, epic, life-changing romance... I’ve always wanted the fairytale… I’ve always wanted it all.<br /><br />It just never seemed like I would get it.<br /><br />For the past few years I've thrown myself into my career as a museum curator. I’m the best of the best, the person every museum wants to hire, so when an opportunity came up to move to Seattle, I jumped at the chance. My cousin and my best friend lived in Seattle and I needed a change. <br /><br />I needed a new beginning.<br /><br />I wasn't expecting to meet anyone in the Emerald City. I wasn't expecting to work closely with the reclusive new sculptor my all-important gallery design was centered around. And I certainly wasn't expecting to fall for him... heart-stopping, epic, life-changing love...<br />My real life fairytale come true.<br /><br />But, like in every fairytale, there’s a villain, a dark and tortured soul... I just didn't know that the villain and the hero in my story would end up being one and the same.<br /><br /><i>New Adult Romance Novel—contains adult content, sexual situations and mature topics. Suited for ages 18 and up.</i></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1035231280?book_show_action=true">Aug 24, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1035231280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14660338121532812742"><b>5+ ‘my hope, my light’ stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/ac1a9898-97eb-439c-921a-175aad033af9_zps7i6vngnh.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296427.jpg' alt=' photo ac1a9898-97eb-439c-921a-175aad033af9_zps7i6vngnh.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Tillie Cole presses my love buttons like no other author. She makes her way right to the top of my favorites list with every beautiful, emotional and stunning story she tells. Her writing is completely captivating and her stories move me like no other. I really thought there was no way any of the ‘Sweet Home’ books could compare to <i>Sweet Fall</i> for me. That book is so special and will always hold a place in my heart. I can happily say that this book was just as goo</span>
  <span id="freeText14660338121532812742" style="display:none"><b>5+ ‘my hope, my light’ stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/ac1a9898-97eb-439c-921a-175aad033af9_zps7i6vngnh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296427.jpg" alt=" photo ac1a9898-97eb-439c-921a-175aad033af9_zps7i6vngnh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tillie Cole presses my love buttons like no other author. She makes her way right to the top of my favorites list with every beautiful, emotional and stunning story she tells. Her writing is completely captivating and her stories move me like no other. I really thought there was no way any of the ‘Sweet Home’ books could compare to <i>Sweet Fall</i> for me. That book is so special and will always hold a place in my heart. I can happily say that this book was just as good as <i>Sweet Fall</i>. Just as beautiful, just as heart wrenching and just as moving. It wrecked me in the best possible way.<br><br>Ally Prince is now an art curator. It’s her dream job. And she just got the opportunity of a lifetime. To work with an artist that moves her. That she’s admired for a long time. For Elpidio. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/bd589383-423d-40de-8fd8-8a8487ed797b_zps3dsor7mn.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296428.jpg" alt=" photo bd589383-423d-40de-8fd8-8a8487ed797b_zps3dsor7mn.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Elpi is a man who’s made a lot of mistakes. He’s a broken hero. He’s trying to make changes in his life. Trying to redeem himself for the things he’s done in his past. He’s not sure if he can ever really make up for the wrong doings in his life, but he’s trying. He expresses his pain, his guilt, and all the things from his past he wants to remember and wants to forget through his sculptures. When he decides to show them, he wants it to be anonymous, hence the name Elpi. He never wants anyone to see him or know him as Elpi. But Ally does. She works her way in. <br><i>
  <blockquote>He was… dark. There was no other adjective I could think of to do him justice. Dark, aggressively tattooed, and absolutely yet unconventionally… beautiful.</blockquote>
</i><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/d921a22c-d0fe-4035-aa04-28834ae31569_zpspnvrqi3z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296429.jpg" alt=" photo d921a22c-d0fe-4035-aa04-28834ae31569_zpspnvrqi3z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>For the first time ever, someone was sharing in this pain with me. A virtual stranger. And I didn’t know what the hell to do with how damn good that felt. I’d vowed to never let anyone in. I didn’t understand why I’d broken that vow with her.</blockquote>
</b><br>Give me a broken boy, a damaged man and I am a happy reader. Elpi is so broken from his past. He has so much darkness he just wants to be free of. He wants to move on with his life and get over the things that have happened but becoming free from your past is not an easy task. He’s been living in darkness for so long. But now that Ally is in his life, now that he’s finally connected to someone for the first time in years, he has some light in the darkness. Some hope.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/68ac6bbb-7be3-4cc8-9930-81c16f15ea52_zpsvkrvj1in.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296430.jpg" alt=" photo 68ac6bbb-7be3-4cc8-9930-81c16f15ea52_zpsvkrvj1in.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>She was fucking perfection. She was light. A blazing golden light. When you’re locked in perpetual darkness, you’ll do anything to fucking chase that light.</blockquote>
</i> I loved the broken hero in this story, but I’m going to just take a moment and completely gush over this heroine. Ally Prince is someone special. She is strong, she is sweet, she is compassionate and she see’s beyond the exterior. She sees the person Elpi is within. She is able to make him see his worth when no one else in the world can. She is able to pull him out of this darkness for a while. She made my heart happy. I love this heroine so much. She is the absolute best. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You are worth your weight in gold, Elpi. You are someone, someone real special.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/499f8eda-35d4-4806-b0c5-f26e75713b5a_zpsq9lqi4pa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296431.jpg" alt=" photo 499f8eda-35d4-4806-b0c5-f26e75713b5a_zpsq9lqi4pa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Sweet Hope</i> is a gorgeous romance, but it is so much more than that. It’s a story of healing. Of guilt, forgiveness, moving forward and acceptance. It’s a story of hope. This is a story that touched my heart. It’s been days since I’ve read and I can’t get it off my mind. I can’t wait for everyone else to read and really ‘meet’ Ally and Elpi. Yes, you see them in the other 3 books, but you don’t really know either of them. How beautiful their hearts are and the people they really are. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/2c810fbf-1bbe-4410-b5d1-2ab021c1ae8f_zps79mfxzcb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296432.jpg" alt=" photo 2c810fbf-1bbe-4410-b5d1-2ab021c1ae8f_zps79mfxzcb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Sweet Hope</i> is not a standalone. You should (at least) read <i>Sweet Fall</i> before you read this. If not the entire series. Trust me, they are worth while reads. This is a series that is just fantastic. I love all the books so much. I loved reading this and seeing all my favorite characters from the previous books. It made me so happy to see them all together and thriving. <br><br>I feel like I’m writing my own little book here so I’ll wrap it up. If you haven’t read this series <b>read it!</b>. And as soon as you do <b>READ THIS BOOK</b>! Another stunning story going to the top of my favorites list! <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I always wanted this. I always wanted this kind of love, this intense love… I just never realized it could be so much more… until you.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/761d4224-9005-41ea-84ac-19833b70b01a_zpsuqbqhoyv.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427620221i/14296433.jpg" alt=" photo 761d4224-9005-41ea-84ac-19833b70b01a_zpsuqbqhoyv.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14660338121532812742" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1050933866" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1050933866" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1050933866?book_show_action=true">Sep 10, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25245349-sweet-hope">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1050933866" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3489496577167640130"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>"You are my hope, Ally. You're every hope I've ever dared to have...la mia luce."</b>
</i><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/e445d49659e8edfa9a9fcd44dcfc1ee1_zpsq2zc60ul.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428197548i/14385973._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo e445d49659e8edfa9a9fcd44dcfc1ee1_zpsq2zc60ul.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>I went into this book with low expectations after seeing several negative reviews. I also was hoping that the guy I despised from <b>"Sweet Fall"</b>, was not going to be the love interest for Ally. I always liked Ally and hoped she would get a kick ass love interest. Well, to my utter surprise Mr Axel Carillo "aka" <b>Elpi</b>, was the PERFECT man for her!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>The entire time I read this, I kept waiting </span>
  <span id="freeText3489496577167640130" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"You are my hope, Ally. You're every hope I've ever dared to have...la mia luce."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/e445d49659e8edfa9a9fcd44dcfc1ee1_zpsq2zc60ul.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428197548i/14385973._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo e445d49659e8edfa9a9fcd44dcfc1ee1_zpsq2zc60ul.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>I went into this book with low expectations after seeing several negative reviews. I also was hoping that the guy I despised from <b>"Sweet Fall"</b>, was not going to be the love interest for Ally. I always liked Ally and hoped she would get a kick ass love interest. Well, to my utter surprise Mr Axel Carillo "aka" <b>Elpi</b>, was the PERFECT man for her!!!<br><br><br><br><br>The entire time I read this, I kept waiting for something to get on my nerves. It never happened. Yes, there is a lot of crying going on, but there were so many valid reasons for the tears. Elpi really made a mess of his life and almost ruined the lives of his two younger brothers. Add on top of that, the fact that he wasn't there when his momma died, this man has so much pain and guilt that he carries with him wherever he goes. He doesn't think he's worthy of redemption. <br><br><br><br><br>Tillie Cole is an amazing author because she made me completely forgive Axel. Once you learn of his suffering and all the things he did to try to protect his mom and little brothers, you can't help but fall for him. He also ends up learning how to sculpt while in prison. His marble sculptures get discovered by a very famous artist, who helps Elpi become somewhat of a celebrity in the art community. Ally is an art curator and is also one of Elpi's biggest fans. She lands the job as the art curator for Elpi's upcoming showcase in Seattle.<br><br><br><br><br>Ally and Elpi have an instant attraction to each other. Although Elpi tried to fight his feelings for Ally, he really never stood a chance. She ends up being his light, his hope. These two have some of the steamiest scenes ever.<b>69</b> anyone???!!<br><br><br><br><br>So I thought what should I rate this book when I finished. I honestly enjoyed the entire story and I even shed a few tears. So many scenes grabbed a hold of my heart. I was rooting for Axel to have the loving bond with his brothers that they had when they were younger. I loved seeing the complete transformation of Axel and the Epilogue wrapped everything up so beautifully. This book gave me so many "feels" that I couldn't justify giving it anything less than a five star rating.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3489496577167640130" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1044108695" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1044108695" />
    <a title="Mysza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza"><img alt="Mysza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1433922560p2/14262653.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1044108695?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mysza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mysza" href="/user/show/14262653-mysza">Mysza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1044108695" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11570241726540153768"> <b>
  <i>** 2,5 stars overall **</i>
</b><br/><br/> <b>
  <i>***** 5 stars for the story *****</i>
</b><br/> <b>
  <i>* 1 star for the writing *</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427998169ra/14349215.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>No, for real...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427998169ra/14349216.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Because it was such a great series, I loved first 3 books and this one, to my utter astonishment, was such a disappointment. The story was powerful, it had great potential, it could have been brilliant. The reclusive, talented artist, trying so much to redeem himself, regretting his sins and all the wrongs he did, to the point that he didn't want anyone to know his identity because he </span>
  <span id="freeText11570241726540153768" style="display:none"> <b>
  <i>** 2,5 stars overall **</i>
</b><br><br> <b>
  <i>***** 5 stars for the story *****</i>
</b><br> <b>
  <i>* 1 star for the writing *</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427998169ra/14349215.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No, for real...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427998169ra/14349216.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Because it was such a great series, I loved first 3 books and this one, to my utter astonishment, was such a disappointment. The story was powerful, it had great potential, it could have been brilliant. The reclusive, talented artist, trying so much to redeem himself, regretting his sins and all the wrongs he did, to the point that he didn't want anyone to know his identity because he felt he didn't deserve any attention, praise or a good word. The idea was excellent and this book could have been solid 5 star for me, if only written differently.<br><br>First, I think it was way too cheesy for my taste. The author probably wanted it to be perfect, but instead, I think she overdid it. Ok, Ally was his and he was hers lightning, <i>la mia luce</i>, their hearts and souls were fused, I get it, but when I'm reading about it for the tenth time, the shit gets old, you know? <br><br>Second, I can't understand a thing in Italian or Spanish for that matter and constant googling phrases started to get on my nerves...<br><br>Third, the crying, OMG, the crying, for real, why so much crying?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427998169i/14349217.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409672858ra/11006911.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/590362.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427998750ra/14349329.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427998750ra/14349331.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the beginning, I thought "Ok, they are pretty emotional, I can deal." <br>And then "Oh, they really cry a lot" <br>And then "Shit, can they stop already?" <br>And then "For fucks sake, that's enough."<br>I am not exaggerating, at the end it was unbearable, I hardly finished. They cried in almost every paragraph the last 20% of the book. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381800902ra/5313529.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I'm just wondering, were there any beta readers? And if so, hell, I wouldn't want betas like that. It's simply not possible not to notice this thing while reading and not telling the author that it is a huge mistake. It's like not telling your girlfriend that she has lipstick on her teeth.<br><br>It makes me sad, because as I said before, the story was strong and the book could have been epic, but somewhere along the way the author exaggerated with big words and the crying fest. <br>Now, I just want a redo! <br><br>PS. I checked, the word "tear" was used 114 times in the book! Just sayin'....<br><br><b>
  <i>Buddy read with lovely Nikki, Jennifer, Brandi and Leslie. &lt;3</i>
</b><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="11570241726540153768" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1135109972" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1135109972" />

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14555400649636459947"><b>5 Redeeming Stars.</b>	<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427754052i/14317521.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ally is a curator that fell in love with a sculptor work before meeting the artist himself. Hired to be the curator of his work in a exhibition in Seattle, she finally meets the man behind the art. And she falls in love with the broken and guilt-driven Elpidio. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427754052i/14317522._SY540_.jpg' width='350' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Elpidio had a bad past, full of mistakes and bad-decisions. And although those decisions were made out of love and concern he strongly believes that aren’t enough rights in the world to ease his wrongs. When he meets </span>
  <span id="freeText14555400649636459947" style="display:none"><b>5 Redeeming Stars.</b>	<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427754052i/14317521.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ally is a curator that fell in love with a sculptor work before meeting the artist himself. Hired to be the curator of his work in a exhibition in Seattle, she finally meets the man behind the art. And she falls in love with the broken and guilt-driven Elpidio. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427754052i/14317522._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Elpidio had a bad past, full of mistakes and bad-decisions. And although those decisions were made out of love and concern he strongly believes that aren’t enough rights in the world to ease his wrongs. When he meets Ally, the first person who truly understands him and his work, for the first time in his dark life he starts to see the light. But with their lives more entwined than they thought and with his ghosts still chasing him, how can he hold on to the hope that the only person who loved him in years and he loves back, will not run way when she found out who he was? <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427754052i/14317523._SY540_.jpg" width="350" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can’t even begin to describe this book. Probably with the fact that made me very happy to find out that Elpidio was who I suspected him to be. I loved Ally in the former books so I was really excited about reading her story, and she did not disappoint. Yes, there was times when the story was a bit cheesy and cliché, but it wrapped up so well that you almost don’t notice it. In an amazingly written and engaging prose, this series end with a mix of feelings of fulfillment, happiness, and sadness in the knowledge that this book is the end of an era. But don't you worry, it ends with an amazing epilogue that will bring you to tears. (Any chance we can have little Levi story?) <br>If you haven’t start this series yet I strongly advise you to start now, you’re missing out in a set of utterly remarkable love stories. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422226870i/13474212.jpg" width="350" height="120" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 5 Stars. <br> <b>Characters Development: </b> I loved Ally! I mean, I had already love her in the previous books, but seeing her now, strong, sweet and confident it was great. She was truly an amazing heroine and her "happy &amp; bubbly" personality complemented perfectly Elpidio's dark one. <br>Elpidio was also a pretty good hero. It was almost hard to see all the guilt he bear because of his past, how broken he was. But it was equally amazing seeing him slowly come to life again. I loved how he got to see more of the others and all they all become a strong family. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>Sensible Subjects: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Violence. Drugs. REALLY low self-worth. Want more?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>Love Triangle: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ No.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1230959195" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230959195" />
    <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei"><img alt="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421992465p2/2551178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1230959195?book_show_action=true">Mar 18, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Vigilante (Feifei)" href="/user/show/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei">Lady Vigilante (Feifei)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=bad-boys">bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=sweet-hero">sweet-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=cheese-puffs">cheese-puffs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=new-adult-express">new-adult-express</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=contemporary-duckie">contemporary-duckie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=i-trust-my-friends">i-trust-my-friends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2551178-lady-vigilante-feifei?shelf=read-to-review">read-to-review</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1230959195" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9455733158489696176"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427662474i/14303911._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>One of my favorite books from last year was book 3 in this series <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___3_' title='Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Fall</a> and though I was completely happy with that book, a few plot events that happened there made me see that a certain side character was practically screaming for a book, so I’m ecstatic that the author decided to write this one. But before I say anything else I have to stress that this book is <i>not</i> meant to be read as a standalone. You must read at least Sweet Fall beforehand. Now back to Sweet Hope...<br/><br/>I liked thi</span>
  <span id="freeText9455733158489696176" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427662474i/14303911._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of my favorite books from last year was book 3 in this series <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___3_" title="Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Fall</a> and though I was completely happy with that book, a few plot events that happened there made me see that a certain side character was practically screaming for a book, so I’m ecstatic that the author decided to write this one. But before I say anything else I have to stress that this book is <i>not</i> meant to be read as a standalone. You must read at least Sweet Fall beforehand. Now back to Sweet Hope...<br><br>I liked this book. It’s a passionate romance story that made my heart pound and had a sweet and loving heroine and a tormented, mysterious hero. Add that with this author’s great writing and the wonderful cast of side characters from previous books it really made this story shine. Along the way, I did take note of little things that were bothersome but at that point, it didn’t affect my enjoyment of the book much. In hindsight, I should’ve realized that all of these little things would accumulate and once I actually hit something I really didn’t like (which happened in the 2nd half of the book), they would become major problems for me because that’s what ended up happening. <br><br>The book started off strong – I love character-driven stories and this was definitely one of them. The heroine Ally Prince is a woman with ambitious career goals and she’s determined to curate an art display for the artist she’s long admired – the hero Elpidio. Even though she’s in love with his work, she’s even more intrigued with the man behind it. Quick observation here: it’s probably just me, but it was a little disturbing to read just how obsessed she was when she never met the guy prior to the exhibit. But in the end, I let that one slide because I can see why she was so fascinated – whenever Elpidio entered the scene, everything just got intense and I couldn’t help but be drawn to this man who was so tormented and could only communicate his emotions through his magnificent sculptures. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427662474i/14303912._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I think what made this book for me was Elpidio. Ally was a perfectly likable heroine and complemented his dark personality with her light, bubbly one, but I’m a sucker for ‘fallen angel’ characters and that’s exactly who Elpidio was. He’s made really, really bad choices in his past that he now regrets and has gone through so much it’s a wonder the man is still alive and kicking. But deep down, he’s just a guy who wanted nothing more than to protect his family and loved ones, and if playing dirty would keep them safe, he’d do it in a heartbeat. <br><br>The romance here definitely felt instantaneous to me, but I loved it anyways because the author wrote it in a way there were no doubts that Ally and Elpidio were each other’s soul mates. However, some events and plot devices happened soon that I wasn’t a fan of, and dragged down my rating:<br><br><b>
  <u>The timeline was all over the place.</u>
</b> While I didn’t have trouble keeping track where the story was at a certain point, I didn’t like the multiple time jumps. Combine that with the occasional flashback scene and I got annoyed by the time I was near the end of the book. This issue isn’t something I’m complaining about just for this book – just like some readers can’t stand cheating, I can’t stand time gaps, especially not ones where chapters in the story started off with ‘a few weeks later,’ ‘a year later,’ ‘fifteen years later,’ etc…Bottom line is, I like continuity in my stories. <br><br><b>
  <u>Major character stupidity.</u>
</b> Okay...this is the main problem I had with Elpidio and other side characters in the second half of the book. To avoid plot spoilers, I won’t list out the exact details but the root of the problem is miscommunication that drove a wedge between these characters and of course, running away is the first solution which leads to even more drama. This was in the final quarter of the book and at this point I kept thinking to myself haven’t these people gone through enough already?! Just get on with the romance!<br><br>From book 3 I already had a soft spot for the Carillo brothers (especially Austin), and seeing them in here at one crucial scene near the end made me cry. The epilogue was also one of the most beautiful book endings I’ve read and really wrapped up this story along with the entire series. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427662474i/14303913._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for my rating, I wavered between 3.5 and 4 because I seriously adored this hero but wasn’t a fan of how the author executed the story from the halfway mark and on. In the end, I’m going with 3.5 stars as I did like it and would still recommend it but it didn’t leave an as memorable impression on me like Sweet Fall did.<br><br><u>Sweet Hope</u> is the final book in the Sweet Home series. You must read Sweet Fall first as the plot and characters are closely connected. <br><br><i>ARC provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i><br><br>P.S. I also think these characters cried too much but that's just me!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9455733158489696176" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1232564981" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15573925036042350332">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars ★★★★★ ♡TOP READ of 2015♡<br/><br/>Now LIVE! <br/>Amazon - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1He0qqo'>http://amzn.to/1He0qqo</a><br/>Amazon UK - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1He0uXq'>http://amzn.to/1He0uXq</a><br/></b> <br/><i>SPOILER FREE REVIEW</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>"The most beautiful art is often born from the most desperate of circumstances."</b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427631310i/14298370._SY540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ally Prince is a 27 years old museum curator. She lives for her love of art and when she lands her dream job curating an exhibition by her favourite artist, modern sculptor Elpidio, she is beyond happy and excited to be given the opportunity to showcase his sculptures after admiring</span>
  <span id="freeText15573925036042350332" style="display:none">★★★★★ <b>5 Stars ★★★★★ ♡TOP READ of 2015♡<br><br>Now LIVE! <br>Amazon - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1He0qqo">http://amzn.to/1He0qqo</a><br>Amazon UK - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1He0uXq">http://amzn.to/1He0uXq</a><br></b> <br><i>SPOILER FREE REVIEW</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The most beautiful art is often born from the most desperate of circumstances."</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427631310i/14298370._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ally Prince is a 27 years old museum curator. She lives for her love of art and when she lands her dream job curating an exhibition by her favourite artist, modern sculptor Elpidio, she is beyond happy and excited to be given the opportunity to showcase his sculptures after admiring them for so long.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"His works... They are both the saddest and most beautiful pieces of art I have ever seen.<br>Every curve of the marble comes from deep within the heart."</b>
</blockquote><br>She flies from her home in LA and goes to stay with her cousin Rome and best friend Molly in Seattle, where the exhibition will take place.<br><br>Elpidio is a lonely and reclusive man who learnt his craft in prison. He sculpts to help curb the anger that lives inside his soul. When his mentor Vin Galanti arranges for his work to appear in a début exhibition, he is reluctant to share his pain and grief that his pieces represent, but when he discovers that the show will take place in Seattle, he decides that maybe it's the perfect time to face his past. - he has family that he let down terribly and needs to make amends with.<br><br>Elpi is lurking in the shadows watching the beautiful curator Aliyana Lucia arrange his sculptures in such a reverent way when he is spotted, something he never intended to happen, but Ally is determined to find out what inspired such sad and beautiful art. She simply cannot let him slink away and he can't seem to find it in him to escape her either.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Fuck porn. A chick as hot as Aliyana Lucia sitting in front of me, hair ruffled in a messy knot and shirt gaping, talking to me in Spanish was the hottest thing I'd ever fucking seen."</b>
</blockquote><br>They find themselves meeting every night in the cover of darkness, to talk about the art but discover they connect on a deeper level, which surprises them both.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"He's the most inspiring, courageous, beautifully dark, tortured, talented sculptor I've ever encountered..."</b>
</blockquote><br>It's not long before they both discover that Elpidio and Aliyana are not quite who they made out to be and Ally discovers that not only was she unintentionally hiding her identity, but Elpidio was most definitely not the man she thought he was. The only trouble is, it may be too late now that he has taken root in her heart.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427631205i/14298344.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>_ _ _ _<br><br><b>This book was so much more than a simple love story,</b> it touched me so deeply how Elpi was so truly broken by his past sins, and how Ally vowed to show him that he was a good man who did bad things only to protect his family. She needed him to realise that he didn't know any better, that he was just a child who didn't have any other choices but to do bad things to survive.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427631205i/14298345.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Everything he did as a young teen was to protect and support his brothers. He doesn't believe he deserves anything good in life whatsoever, but Ally gives him the one thing he never imagined he'd have. <i>Hope.</i><br><br>He cannot understand why Ally anything to do with him, he keeps warning her to stay away, that he is trouble and a bad person. <br> <br><blockquote>
  <b>"And even crazier, she loved my work... the twisted, fucked-up sculptures from my mind."</b>
</blockquote><br>But she sees him for the man he is today, a man who loves his family so unconditionally that he couldn't possibly have a black heart. She will fight for him, and <i>with</i> him, to bring him the redemption she believes he deserves.<br><br>For him, she is the light who makes his darkness go away<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"Lei era speranza...She was hope. La mia luce... my light."</b>
</blockquote><br>_ _ _ _<br><br>This book hit me right in the gut, it was so sad but full of hope at the same time. It was the perfect end to this series and by far the <b>best book Tillie has ever written.</b> Get your tissues ready for this one, it was an emotional one but heart-warming at the same time. This is a story about <b>LOVE. FAMILY, HOPE and REDEMPTION.</b><br><br>I loved this book so much, it was just that good and it really touched my heart so deeply.<br><br>Told in dual POV, it is necessary to have read Sweet Fall first in order to truly understand the dynamics of the characters and the back story of Elpidio and Ally.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345-sweet-fall" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Fall Review</a><br><br><i>ARC gratefully received from the author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://ilovebooklove-ab.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228252.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.facebook.com/ilovebooklove" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420460638i/13228250.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katy Loves Romance ❤️" href="/user/show/10247668-katy-loves-romance">Katy Loves Romance ❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10247668-katy-loves-romance?shelf=books-that-make-me-feel-and-cry">books-that-make-me-feel-and-cry</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1161330671" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8311094161389034602"><b>6 Emotional final endings stars******</b><br/><br/><b>This is a spoiler free review but in order to understand this book please read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___3_' title='Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1404121856s/18759345.jpg' alt='Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a> first</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/39F70E6D-8F65-4444-8883-EABC0A3DAFAB_zps7w5xtujr.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427979406i/14345753._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 39F70E6D-8F65-4444-8883-EABC0A3DAFAB_zps7w5xtujr.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This story effected me so deeply I'm not sure if it's because I have read this series pretty recently but for me this was the perfect ending to an <b>Outstanding, Deep and Beautiful series.</b><br/><br/>I was excited to find out more about Ally, the striking and beautiful woman we read in the previous stories. When we read her tid bits from the previous books I saw how beautiful she was o</span>
  <span id="freeText8311094161389034602" style="display:none"><b>6 Emotional final endings stars******</b><br><br><b>This is a spoiler free review but in order to understand this book please read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___3_" title="Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1404121856s/18759345.jpg" alt="Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> first</b><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/39F70E6D-8F65-4444-8883-EABC0A3DAFAB_zps7w5xtujr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427979406i/14345753._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 39F70E6D-8F65-4444-8883-EABC0A3DAFAB_zps7w5xtujr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This story effected me so deeply I'm not sure if it's because I have read this series pretty recently but for me this was the perfect ending to an <b>Outstanding, Deep and Beautiful series.</b><br><br>I was excited to find out more about Ally, the striking and beautiful woman we read in the previous stories. When we read her tid bits from the previous books I saw how beautiful she was on the inside <b>(giving the extra mile)</b> as well as on the outside, yet she was lonely and wanted what her friends had. She didn't just want a relationship but she wanted to <b>NEED</b> her man, she wanted something deeper something that was for her and in that this story is about a true love a story that through unlikely sources finds something deeper and something that from the outside people judge yet from the inside is right. <br><br>Ally is an art curator, she is there at forefront to work with the artists to make the pieces look right, to make them look how the audience should see them for the beauty they are. She is employed to design the work of sculpture artist Elpido the reclusive who she has followed for years the artist no-one has ever met who knows nothing about, this is her dream job and here she is taking this opportunity with both hands to create something that will make Elpido proud of his work. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/CF139E84-4DBE-4FDA-895C-3C9D43C6ACC5_zpsoreokf6e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427979406i/14345754._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo CF139E84-4DBE-4FDA-895C-3C9D43C6ACC5_zpsoreokf6e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Elpi is a dark soul and comes to the gallery at night only to see how things are progressing in that Ally bumps into him, and slowly Ally begins to strip Eli of his troubles and try and understand what the pain in his pieces are all about. At night they begin to gain a friendship based on their loneliness.<br><br>Ally has watched her cousin (Rome) and best friend (Molly) fall in love and wants that for herself, she never expected to start to fall for a man that has a dark past yet she keeps going back to Elpi because there is just something so very special about him, something unique and different and something <b>That she desperately wants.</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/27CDE83A-FD90-4F94-9D87-6A15026A283C_zpspatka4bs.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427979406i/14345755._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 27CDE83A-FD90-4F94-9D87-6A15026A283C_zpspatka4bs.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Elpi has a darker past full of pain and he has done things that he's not proud of he is a broken man, a sinful man, a man that he thinks Ally should stay away from but again Elpi finds himself craving Ally likewise he has never felt like this before. These are two souls that want and crave each other, two people that find something in each other that nobody else can or has ever given them. Ally is Elpis light and what Elpi doesn't understand is Elpi is the same for Ally you can't help who you fall for. This is such a beautiful story about hope and chances about finding the right person for ourselves its about giving life a chance, giving ourselves a chance to breathe and believe that there is goodness in people who may look on the outside dangerous yet on the inside have hearts of gold. <br><br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/6A59F4B5-3FE5-499E-B6AE-6139DBFCD0BB_zpsm8d3yckb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427979406i/14345756._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 6A59F4B5-3FE5-499E-B6AE-6139DBFCD0BB_zpsm8d3yckb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>This was a character driven story about possibilities, about family friendships and <b>LOVE</b> a different raw kind of love and these slightly darker stories are always worth the read in my opinion I connect to them much deeper but that's just me. <br><br><a href="http://s1298.photobucket.com/user/ktdunning/media/book%20collages/D669516D-B24D-48F0-923B-CF90C4BEB924_zpsy4mtd7ec.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427979406i/14345757._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo D669516D-B24D-48F0-923B-CF90C4BEB924_zpsy4mtd7ec.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>I urge anyone who hasn't started to read this series to start and give it a chance because for me this one of the best NA romances out there. I will forever keep all these characters close to my heart. Thank you Tillie for giving us stories that mean something for giving us something to think about something to cherish for giving us LOVE and for endings and healing I LOVED EVERY DAMN WORD, but most of all thank you for giving us characters that gripped my every core and made me <b>FEEL.</b> <br><br><b>That is all and thanks for reading my emotional review.</b> <br><br><b>Read my Reviews for the rest of the series</b><br><b>SWEET HOME</b> ~ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1P2T2nt">http://bit.ly/1P2T2nt</a><br><b>SWEET ROME</b> ~ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1I7N1DX">http://bit.ly/1I7N1DX</a><br><b>SWEET FALL</b> ~ <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://bit.ly/1F6vKF8">http://bit.ly/1F6vKF8</a><br><br><i>ARC gifted via Have Book Will Read in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8311094161389034602" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_842431124" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/842431124" />
    <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle"><img alt="Jennifer Kyle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514915429p2/9916227.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/842431124?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer Kyle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer Kyle" href="/user/show/9916227-jennifer-kyle">Jennifer Kyle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer842431124" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15871344038181155423"><br/><b>3.5 Stars </b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Hope is a fervent, silent wish that everything will turn out just as you dream…”</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427731423i/14314072._SX540_.jpg' width='390' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I <b>LOVE</b> this series but this story was a bit too cheesy and predictable for my tastes and not as gritty as I expected. Ally is a terrific character and I was so excited that her time to find love has arrived. Having it be with a hot broken artist to boot was a total extra bonus. (Speaking of his work, Colleen Hoover ruined me because I totally expected to see pictures of these pieces in this book.) <br/><br/>Ally</span>
  <span id="freeText15871344038181155423" style="display:none"><br><b>3.5 Stars </b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Hope is a fervent, silent wish that everything will turn out just as you dream…”</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427731423i/14314072._SX540_.jpg" width="390" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> this series but this story was a bit too cheesy and predictable for my tastes and not as gritty as I expected. Ally is a terrific character and I was so excited that her time to find love has arrived. Having it be with a hot broken artist to boot was a total extra bonus. (Speaking of his work, Colleen Hoover ruined me because I totally expected to see pictures of these pieces in this book.) <br><br>Ally is taken with Elpi’s work and stoked to be his curator for his first showing in Seattle. She flies out from New York to stay with Rome and Molly and get working on her dream job. Her deep feelings for each of his sculptures and excitement was fantastic. The artist and Ally’s connection and scenes were hot and steamy...still a bit farfetched how they got together in the first place (I kept waiting for Vic’s connection to the group- like a professor from Bama or something). All the art work was very well described as were this couples scenes together in his studio and the love they find in one another.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>I must be pretty cold hearted because there was way too much character crying going on in this story…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1491908016ra/22459851.gif" width="390" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Still some scenes did yank on my heartstrings and I loved the family aspect of the story. Ally and Elpi’s relationship was sweet and how it affected the cast of characters in this series. At times the story was over the top dramatic and just didn’t wow me. However, I’m a huge fan of this series well beyond their years with Bama and would not be opposed to another book!<br><br> <b>
  <i> “You’re not the villain in this story, you’re the beautifully flawed hero. You’re the dark hero who has been sacrificing himself all along.”</i>
</b><br><br>Thanks for the Buddy Read <b>Mysza, Brandi, Nikki &amp; Leslie</b> <br>❤ You Girls!</span>

<div id="review_1025244231" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1025244231" />
    <a title="Eliza" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15220898-eliza"><img alt="Eliza" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588523539p2/15220898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1025244231?book_show_action=true">Aug 12, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eliza" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eliza" href="/user/show/15220898-eliza">Eliza</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=sweetheart">sweetheart</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=i-pictured-it">i-pictured-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15220898-eliza?shelf=right-in-the-feels">right-in-the-feels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1025244231" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10802650922398233680"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Title:</b> Sweet Hope<br/><b>Series:</b> Sweet Home,#4<br/><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br/><b>Release date: </b> 29th March, 2015<br/><b>Rating:</b> 3.5-4 "Lighting" stars<br/><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br/><b> HEA: </b> <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[ Yes  <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg' width='400' height='40' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427628709i/14297933._SY540_.jpg' width='400' alt=' photo 016E2F4F-0A14-4310-A64A-90B615EE4A32_zpst36uwzgd.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Every time I read a book from Tillie Cole's Sweet Home Series it pretty much guarantees there will be an abundance of <b>feels</b> and <b>tears</b>. Sweet Hope does not disappoint, on this occasion the mass of emotion comes courtesy of Ally and Elpidio. Ally's role so far in this series has been that of sweet, loyal cousin and friend be</span>
  <span id="freeText10802650922398233680" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431890566i/14878986.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Title:</b> Sweet Hope<br><b>Series:</b> Sweet Home,#4<br><b>Author:</b> Tillie Cole<br><b>Release date: </b> 29th March, 2015<br><b>Rating:</b> 3.5-4 "Lighting" stars<br><b>Cliffhanger:</b> No<br><b> HEA: </b> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Yes  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396707796i/9175086.jpg" width="400" height="40" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427628709i/14297933._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt=" photo 016E2F4F-0A14-4310-A64A-90B615EE4A32_zpst36uwzgd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Every time I read a book from Tillie Cole's Sweet Home Series it pretty much guarantees there will be an abundance of <b>feels</b> and <b>tears</b>. Sweet Hope does not disappoint, on this occasion the mass of emotion comes courtesy of Ally and Elpidio. Ally's role so far in this series has been that of sweet, loyal cousin and friend besides that, she's a bit of a mystery and I had been looking forward to learning more about her.<br><br>Working as a curator, Ally has just been afforded the opportunity that not only will be of professional development to her but also personally inspiring. The Artist in question is the mysterious Elpidio. Having followed and studied his work previously it's important to her to understand the man behind his creations. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427641615i/14300206._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt=" photo C70FCCD5-E1BF-4D5A-8E03-6B331D0D5904_zpsw4fbun31.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Elpi is a tortured individual so weighed down by tremendous guilt and the mistakes of his past, he refuses to see any of the goodness Ally sees in him. She is the smooth to his rough edges, the light to his darkness. Rather than repel her, he speaks to her soul. Her faith in him is unrelenting. It's impossible to not warm to Ally, she becomes his main source of positivity and as a reader their best interests became mine. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427652047i/14301673._SY540_.jpg" width="400" alt=" photo 1C1F5F4C-05F1-4A03-9A62-E4B38044D118_zpsccmmbb4y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The professional relationship blurs and sculpts into a a physical and emotional one. It's guilty of being a little corny at times and I dare say too intense for my fragile nature at times too. I would have liked to have seen some lighter times between them but at the same time I recognise the authors ability of staying honest to the story. To understand the depth of Sweet Hope you have to read Sweet Fall but I say, this series is too great to not read them all.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427666925i/14304506._SX540_.jpg" width="400" alt=" photo 8D80F14F-0FE8-4BD8-87E5-0D368D92E223_zpsh0pnbzgk.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>FOLLOW SMOKIN HOT BOOK BLOG ON: <b><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/BlogSmokin/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img alt="Twitter"     <a title="Brandi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi"><img alt="Brandi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384348451p2/5494655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1049283634?book_show_action=true">Sep 08, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1049283634" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer495031134466099734"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427739934i/14315559._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This has been an enjoyable series, with <i>Sweet Fall</i> being my favorite. Ally and Elpidio story made for a quick read, but maybe a little to sappy for me. There was some instalove and a fair amount of cheesiness. That said, it was easy to pull for Ally and Elpi, I enjoyed both characters. And Elpi, my heart broke for him a few times, but overall the story was a little too predictable. So while it had its moments, this wasn't an epic story for me. It was nice to catch up with the Sweet Home</span>
  <span id="freeText495031134466099734" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427739934i/14315559._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This has been an enjoyable series, with <i>Sweet Fall</i> being my favorite. Ally and Elpidio story made for a quick read, but maybe a little to sappy for me. There was some instalove and a fair amount of cheesiness. That said, it was easy to pull for Ally and Elpi, I enjoyed both characters. And Elpi, my heart broke for him a few times, but overall the story was a little too predictable. So while it had its moments, this wasn't an epic story for me. It was nice to catch up with the Sweet Home gang, but these people were constantly crying, and it drove me nuts. Seriously, someone always had tears in their eyes, or running down their face...and I guess I'm an unfeeling bitch, because not one tear did I shed. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427737818ra/14315286.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Thanks, Jennifer, Mysza, Nikki, and Leslie for the BR. &lt;33</b></span>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1202012151" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1202012151" />
    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1202012151?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1202012151" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18315794301034491576"><br/>There is just something so beautiful and unique about Tillie’s writing. Whether it’s a motorcycle club, a college football player, or an troubled artist I can’t help but fall in love. <br/><br/>I have liked Ally since we first met her in Sweet Home. She was the beautiful, popular cheerleader who was just a good person. She loves her friends, family and is crazy loyal, so I couldn’t wait to finally read her story. Speculating and guessing as to who her mystery guy would be was half the fun and I was so ple</span>
  <span id="freeText18315794301034491576" style="display:none"><br>There is just something so beautiful and unique about Tillie’s writing. Whether it’s a motorcycle club, a college football player, or an troubled artist I can’t help but fall in love. <br><br>I have liked Ally since we first met her in Sweet Home. She was the beautiful, popular cheerleader who was just a good person. She loves her friends, family and is crazy loyal, so I couldn’t wait to finally read her story. Speculating and guessing as to who her mystery guy would be was half the fun and I was so pleased to learn who her love interest would be. <br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>I had an insatiable need to know more. I didn’t know Elpidio, not at all. But something inside me wanted to help him heal.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>Elpidio is a famous artist, but no one knows the man behind his alias. Ally is so excited when she lands the curator position for his show in Seattle. His pieces have inspired and evoked so much emotion in her, and she is in love with his work before she ever lays eyes on the man behind it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428021302i/14352214._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It is an odd feeling to have fans who love and adore you when you hate yourself and that is exactly how Elpidio feels. He doesn’t feel comfortable with his success, but it’s an unstoppable force. Like most artist, he didn’t get into art for the money or fame, it’s his way of working through his many emotions, mainly regret and fear. <br><br>When Ally and Elpidio meet for the first time they have no idea their pasts are linked together. It has been a long time and they’re faraway from home. So without any outside influences they are able to get to know each other and form a connection. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>She was fucking perfection. She was light. A blazing golden light. When you’re locked in perpetual darkness, you’ll do anything to fucking chase that light.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>I loved this time they had together, it was sweet and sexy. But what I really enjoyed was the build up, because as the reader you know their connection and can only speculate as to how things will play out. I was on the edge of my seat dying to see what would happen, wanting them to further their connection, but also wanting the truth known…I was torn. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428021302i/14352215._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Sweet Hope</i> broke my heart. I loved every aspect of this story. Seeing them meet and get to know each other was sweet and heartwarming. Then to see the aftermath of their identities, watching them fall apart and deciding on where to go next broke my heart. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>It was the most intense and meaningful moment of my life. Here, deep inside this woman who only knew the man I was now, not the unfeeling bastard I was before, was my more.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>This is a story of redemption, forgiveness and love. Not just love between a man and woman, but love for your family and friends. I loved watching the love story, I mean that’s why I read books, but watching them grow as people had me full of emotions. Seeing the struggles and remains of a relationships, then to see them rebuilt…absolutely beautiful!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428021302i/14352216._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am aware of the intense fan-girling I am doing over this book, but I absolutely love books that make me feel. I love a damaged hero and I love a strong heroine, <i>Sweet Hope</i> had both. I highly recommend this fantastic read. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I always wanted this. I always wanted this kind of love, this intense love… I just never realized it could be so much more… until you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>
  <a href="http://readingissexybookblog.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574955.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
<br>
  <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/Reading-is-Sexy-Book-Blog/717861984979600" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574956.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/13095060-beverly" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574957.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/readingissexybo/" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423003910i/13574958.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
