<div id="review_899732415" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/899732415" />
    <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake"><img alt="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605987751p2/11626803.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/899732415?book_show_action=true">Apr 03, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️" href="/user/show/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake">Val ⚓️ Shameless Non-Snowflake ⚓️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25245349-sweet-hope">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11626803-val-shameless-non-snowflake?shelf=young-adult-new-adult">young-adult-new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer899732415" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6354874796751530518"><b>4 Low Lightning Stars</b><br/><br/>Sooooooo, I have been more than ready for this book for quite some time.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426695653i/14082236._SY540_.jpg' width='312.5' height='342.5' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>As in the moment-I-was-done-with-<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/829405739' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Fall</a>-ready. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424099091ra/13715605.gif' width='420' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The fact that Ally's love interest was kept super secret and mysteriously mentioned in the last book's epilogue? <br/><br/>Color me even <i>more</i> intrigued.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427769314ra/14319274.gif' width='380' height='213' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I made sure not to read ANY reviews of this book before picking it up, because I didn't want to ruin the big "reveal" for myself. <br/><br/>Cause I was super excited.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427769314ra/14319275.gif' width='500' height='375' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So imagine my <s>horror</s> surprise when at 12% in I realize tha</span>
  <span id="freeText6354874796751530518" style="display:none"><b>4 Low Lightning Stars</b><br><br>Sooooooo, I have been more than ready for this book for quite some time.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426695653i/14082236._SY540_.jpg" width="312.5" height="342.5" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As in the moment-I-was-done-with-<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/829405739" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Fall</a>-ready. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424099091ra/13715605.gif" width="420" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The fact that Ally's love interest was kept super secret and mysteriously mentioned in the last book's epilogue? <br><br>Color me even <i>more</i> intrigued.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427769314ra/14319274.gif" width="380" height="213" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I made sure not to read ANY reviews of this book before picking it up, because I didn't want to ruin the big "reveal" for myself. <br><br>Cause I was super excited.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427769314ra/14319275.gif" width="500" height="375" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So imagine my <s>horror</s> surprise when at 12% in I realize that this book really <i>is</i> going to be about...art.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427769314ra/14319276.gif" width="400" height="295" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, there is nothing <i>wrong</i> with art, per say, it's just...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427769314ra/14319277.gif" width="500" height="282" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This...uncertainty was then exponetially heightened when I read that the proposed love interst's name was...<br><br>...<i>Elpidio</i>. <br><br>Which, I'm sorry not sorry, sounds a little too much like <i>epilator</i> - as in - HAIR REMOVAL epilator<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427769314i/14319278._SX540_.jpg" width="736" height="298" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, I know this is probably just me - no one else could possibly be this nucking futs - but, it made it hard for me to get into "certain scenes" when, instead of hearing a name being screamed out in passion, I hear the buzzing of a hair removal tool and have smarting sympathy pain in my arm pits...<br><br>*<br>*<br>*<br>*<br>*<br>*<br>*<br>*<br>*<br>* <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427769314i/14319279._SY540_.jpg" width="425" height="750" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Just sayin.'<br><br><b>But I digress.</b><br><br>Thankfully, Tillie Cole is a goddess and this story ended up being everything I wanted it to be. <br><br>I don't want to get too much into the story line, because I think going into this one blind - not knowing who Ally's man ends up being until it's revealed - really adds something to the story.<br><br>But I will say this:<br><br>This story was about more than art (even though that aspect of the story turned out to be pretty badass).<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The most beautiful art is often born in the most desperate circumstances."</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Now, constant crying and some random OTT-ness aside, this was a book that touched on a lot of good themes. <br><br><b>Making <i>mistakes</i>.<br><br>Seeking <i>forgiveness</i>.<br><br>Wanting <i>redemption</i>.<br><br>Finding <i>hope</i>.<br><br>True <i>friendship</i>.<br><br>True <i>family</i>.<br><br>And, of course <i>true love</i>. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427771437i/14319416.jpg" width="272" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But more than anything it was really fun to catch up with all my favorite Bama friends - especially Rome and Molly.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="6354874796751530518" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1025277903" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1025277903" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1025277903?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1025277903" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer135717554640061407"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427377489i/14266832._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> 5+++ Stars </b><br/><i> PLEASE NOTE: <b>SWEET FALL</b> should be read <b>before</b> reading <b>SWEET HOPE</b> </i><br/><br/><br/><b>‘Lei era speranza…She was hope. La mia luce…my light.’</b><br/><br/>Sweet Hope is one of those stories where if we could give it an infinite number of stars we would. This book is perfection and on an emotional level we don’t read and experience often. The writing is once again of the flawless and evocative calibre that is the signature of Tillie Cole. She grabbed our hearts once more with her words right from the onset and still ha</span>
  <span id="freeText135717554640061407" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427377489i/14266832._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> 5+++ Stars </b><br><i> PLEASE NOTE: <b>SWEET FALL</b> should be read <b>before</b> reading <b>SWEET HOPE</b> </i><br><br><br><b>‘Lei era speranza…She was hope. La mia luce…my light.’</b><br><br>Sweet Hope is one of those stories where if we could give it an infinite number of stars we would. This book is perfection and on an emotional level we don’t read and experience often. The writing is once again of the flawless and evocative calibre that is the signature of Tillie Cole. She grabbed our hearts once more with her words right from the onset and still hasn’t let go. We will never forget this story Sweet Hope has left an incredible impression on our hearts. No words we say can possible do Tillie Cole any justice here.<br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re not the villain in this story, you’re the beautifully flawed hero. You’re the dark hero who has been sacrificing himself all along.”</i>
</b><br><br>Now; we are very aware that this story can be very easy to spoil for future readers. Tillie Cole herself has asked for non-spoiler reviews and we wholeheartedly agree. What a shame it would be for readers not to go into this one ‘blind’. So; we will not talk about the story in any detail, instead we will tell you how we felt. After all we read to feel and be shocked, surprised and overcome with emotion. That is the very essence of why we read and so it should be.<br><br><b>
  <i>“The most beautiful art is often born from the most desperate of circumstances.”</i>
</b><br><br>We had so many phone conversations whilst reading Sweet Hope; it’s the kind of raw almost poetic story that swallows you up and spits you out emotionally exhausted at the end. We both sat reading with constant tears in our eyes and cried on the phone to each other. Many coffees were consumed and yeah both of us got stress headaches from the crying. Did it ease up? No, the emotion overwhelmed us right till the end building steadily to a crescendo that had us on our knees unable to breathe. And you know what? We’d read it again just to feel the power of Tillie Cole’s words.<br><br><b>‘He was living, breathing poetry. Not love poetry, but the poetry which tears out your heart, rips it to shreds, pushes it back into your chest, and makes you question what the hell just obliterated your soul.’</b><br><br>Her characters have such depth and intensity we’ve taken them into our hearts in an everlasting embrace. What a way to finish a series with an epilogue that had us smiling, laughing and crying in equal measure. Heartbreakingly beautiful in every way possible. Surprising and astounding as every single character from this series had us riveted and remembering moments whilst experiencing thoughts and feelings all over again.<b> THIS is why we read – pure book magic.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“…with you…I feel…I feel…everything, every-fucking-thing…right here…”</i>
</b><br><br>Ally is without question one of our favourite heroines in fiction. Her understanding, compassion, intelligence, maturity and capacity for love is immense. She’s a fighter and displays such strength emotionally it was an awe inspiring experience. Her loyalty and passion is unwavering and her beliefs cemented and fought for.<br><br><b>‘She was fucking perfection. She was light. A blazing golden light. When you’re locked in perpetual darkness, you’ll do anything to fucking chase that light.’</b><br><br>When Ally gives her heart it is not done half-heartedly. Ally finds the love she’s been waiting for in the most unlikely of places – she falls for the passion and soul of another. She sees him before being faced with the man himself and it was incredibly powerful.<br><br><b>‘I wanted to forget who I was for a while…at least for tonight. Forget it all. The last few weeks, the last few years…everything…just for a fucking while.’</b><br><br>Elpidio the dangerous and intense mystery, the artist – the broken man who speaks from his soul through his hands. A man with a past so tragic and violent. Our hearts bled for him. His place in the world is one he no longer understands, his past a constant darkness surrounding him. A darkness he doesn’t take lightly and accepts as his fate. His karma. This man stands in the face of adversity – a storm in which he is the eye, knowingly feeling the weight of his actions and their consequences. But this man carries within him a heart-breaking acceptance, a loyalty so fierce brought on by a devoted love and protection. Elpidio brings his entire heart to the table as well as his penance.<br><br><b>
  <i>“His work….it’s my soul. It’s life, death, love, tragedy, and everything in between, every human condition….everything.”</i>
</b><br><br>This love did not come quietly. This love came like a ferocious storm which picked up all the pieces and changed fates forever. A love that spread its wings and enveloped more than just Ally and Elpidio. It was an incredible experience that will stay with us forever. <b>THIS…..this is how you bring your readers to their knees and reminds them why they love to read!</b> A standing ovation by us to Tillie Cole.<br><br><b>
  <i>“He’s my more, my bolt of lightning, the one I’ve been waiting for all my life.”</i>
</b><br><br><i>**Reviewed from an ARC copy provided by the author, with thanks**</i><br><br><b>
  <a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/2014/08/19/sweet-fall-sweet-home-3-by-tillie-cole-review-amazing-giveaway/" rel="nofollow noopener">OUR SWEET FALL REVIEW</a>
</b><br><a href="http://wp.me/p2WbFf-5Hb" rel="nofollow noopener">SWEET HOME REVIEW at TB</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409751100i/11016560._SY540_.jpg" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✦✦✦ TB Blog :<a href="http://totallybookedblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">TotallybookedBlog</a><br>✦✦✦ Come say Hi : <a href="https://www.facebook.com/pages/TotallyBooked/257135974397181%20&lt;br%20/&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Facebook</a><br>✦✦✦Follow us: <a href="https://twitter.com/TotallyBooked1%20&lt;/b&gt;" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Twitter</a><br>✦✦✦Check out: <a href="http://www.pinterest.com/totallybookedb/" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on Pinterest</a> <br>✦✦✦ We're on TSU: <a href="https://www.tsu.co/TBBLOG" rel="nofollow noopener">TB on TSU</a></b><br><br><br><br></span>

<div id="review_1175620216" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1175620216" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1175620216?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1175620216" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17431258741328234705"><b>FINALLY LIVE!!! - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1ESpjVT'>http://amzn.to/1ESpjVT</a></b><br/><br/><b>5 Speranzoso Hopeful Stars</b><br/><br/>I have a girl crush. I’m crushing on Tillie Cole. I get to meet her in May and when I do, I’m going to tackle her and fan-girl hardcore.<br/><br/>I LOVE Tillie Cole’s writing and I LOVE Sweet Hope!!!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Lei era speranza… She was hope. La mia luce… my light.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Sweet Hope is a standalone and is part of the Sweet Home series.<br/><br/>Ally Prince is Romeo’s cousin. All of her friends are married and in love and Ally is still single. She has one pas</span>
  <span id="freeText17431258741328234705" style="display:none"><b>FINALLY LIVE!!! - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1ESpjVT">http://amzn.to/1ESpjVT</a></b><br><br><b>5 Speranzoso Hopeful Stars</b><br><br>I have a girl crush. I’m crushing on Tillie Cole. I get to meet her in May and when I do, I’m going to tackle her and fan-girl hardcore.<br><br>I LOVE Tillie Cole’s writing and I LOVE Sweet Hope!!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Lei era speranza… She was hope. La mia luce… my light.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Sweet Hope is a standalone and is part of the Sweet Home series.<br><br>Ally Prince is Romeo’s cousin. All of her friends are married and in love and Ally is still single. She has one passion and its art. She’s a museum curator and goes to Seattle for her next assignment. It’s also where her friends and family lives.<br>Elpidio is a new artist. He creates exquisite marble sculptures. <br><br>He’s a tortured artist with a gift. He literally hammers his frustrations and agony into his pieces. He doesn’t understand why there’s so much buzz centered on his work. His passion is creating. He’s not obsessed with his work. It’s his form of outlet.<br><br><i>Elpi is the Hero and Villain all in one.</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>You are worth your weight in gold, Elpi. You are someone, someone real special</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love Elpi. I love his darkness, I love his discomfort and I love his reaction towards people. Elpi struggles with moving forward when his past haunts him daily and it’s constantly reminding him of his past actions. He’s recluse, broody and sexy as heck. People should fear Elpi. He doesn’t look like the nice guy, but Ally sees past all that.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>How do you exist in this world without having to fight? Without pain?</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The connection between Ally and Elpi is indescribable. There is not a lot of angst but plenty of tension. It’s an emotionally filled book, but I wouldn’t have it any other way. I enjoyed the inner monologues. I wanted to know what Ally was thinking. I wanted to feel Elpi’s pain and remorse.<br><br>I can’t stress how much I enjoyed Ally and Elpi’s interactions. Ally brings the light towards Elpi’s gloom. I love Ally. She’s a strong Heroine. She stands by her man no matter what and it’s refreshing to see such a resilient character. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She was …perfection. She was light. A blazing golden light. When you’re locked in perpetual darkness, you’ll do anything to …chase that light. La mia luce...</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>As far as I was concerned, I deserved to spend the rest of my life miserable for what I’d done. But here, deep inside the most beautiful woman I’d ever seen, the woman who just got me, I was bartering with God to let me keep her<br>I love the pace. Sweet Hope reads well. It reads straight forward with a few memories sprinkled throughout. I wouldn’t call them flashbacks, but just tiny moments.<br><br>You also get plenty of the gang, Romeo, Molly, Austin and Lexi. They all play a pivotal role in the story and I’m happy to read how much the couples have grown. It’s super cute. <br>Sweet Hope is a beautiful story about regrets, guilt and redemption. I crave these books. I long and lust for these books. Thank you Tillie Cole for writing this brilliant piece. It was perfection.<br><br><i>An ARC was provided in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18105011.Sweet_Home__Sweet_Home___1_" title="Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1376473414s/18105011.jpg" alt="Sweet Home (Sweet Home, #1) by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/969744341" rel="nofollow noopener">REVIEW</a> | <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/149298079X/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=149298079X&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=BSAP5KVL3TVZDZ2B" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20653654.Sweet_Rome__Sweet_Home___2_" title="Sweet Rome (Sweet Home, #2) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1391040867s/20653654.jpg" alt="Sweet Rome (Sweet Home, #2) by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00I4D2QYS/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00I4D2QYS&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20&amp;linkId=JOFV4QZ2VGJNUNYP" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___3_" title="Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1404121856s/18759345.jpg" alt="Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #3) by Tillie Cole" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_1250856294" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1250856294" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1250856294?book_show_action=true">Apr 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Tillie Cole, Romance</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1250856294" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14032006718865559768">4 Because I am a Emotional Mess Stars * * * * <br/><br/>First... Have I given this book lots of stars because it is perfect... Hell no! Were there things which could cause you to think I really have to suspend my disbelief... yes...did I care overall... no. And here is why...I just loved the essence of it all. I had just stayed up and read in one sitting Sweet Fall (<a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1250830986'>https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a>) because in order to appreciate this book... you must read the other. The impact and emotions from t</span>
  <span id="freeText14032006718865559768" style="display:none">4 Because I am a Emotional Mess Stars * * * * <br><br>First... Have I given this book lots of stars because it is perfect... Hell no! Were there things which could cause you to think I really have to suspend my disbelief... yes...did I care overall... no. And here is why...I just loved the essence of it all. I had just stayed up and read in one sitting Sweet Fall (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1250830986">https://www.goodreads.com/review/show...</a>) because in order to appreciate this book... you must read the other. The impact and emotions from that read were still very fresh when starting this, so I was primed and ready for what was to come.<br><br>This is primarily Ally's Love Story but as it unfolds, it becomes much much more. She was always watching all her friends fall in love... the type of can't breathe without you love. Molly and her cousin Rome had it; then came Austin and Lexie. Even Cassie and J.D. fell hard for each other....Fast forward and all the crew are living their lives. Rome is still the outstanding Quarterback for the Seahawks and now Austin has been transferred to be his Wide Receiver again. Lexie and Austin are doing great with Levi growing up and becoming his football star, too. The bros are back, living and playing in Seattle.<br><br>Ally has become one of the top curators in the art world and works with museums all over. She is based in Los Angeles and we catch up with her flying to NYC to meet with a sculpting master who is choosing the person to handle the 1st exhibit of Elpidio. This is an artist she has become passionate about... written articles and books lauding his pure method of hand tools on marble like the masters. She has traveled from one coast to the other for this hour to prove she is the only one to tell his story in this exhibit. Vin, the one who discovered this genius asks Ally why her....and in her answer, we see everything we need to know about her.<br><br>Ally is a pure romantic... caught in the beauty and pain in life and art. She feels and sees things with her heart on her sleeve... she is open to the calling of beauty in all forms, whether be music, painting or sculpture. She has the romance in her blood from her mother's side... a proud Latina...to her soul and purposely used her mother's maiden name as her own to separate herself from the family known for Big Oil. Ally did it by professionally being Aliyana Lucia. She is ready to take on this moment...everything has lead up to this and to have it take place in Seattle is a bonus. She will be able to stay with her dear cousin-in-law/best pal Molly. <br><br>Ally dives in setting up the space for the exhibit. She is overseeing everything to be as perfect as it can be. The pieces are being delivered and with each unwrapping... it is like a rebirth... coming to the light for her eyes and heart to gaze and feel....the pain and darkness coupled with the care and love each piece exudes; it cannot be denied. It is a wonder to her. One night she is surprised by someone in the gallery close to a piece...staring at it...she is nervous and concerned as it is not open to the public. She slowly makes herself known and explains the man should not be there...He turns, looks at her and runs out the door. She checks with the security guard and it turns out, the elusive Elpidio has been coming by at midnight every night.<br><br>Stunned, she mentally kicks herself and makes sure to be there the next night. Again, he shows and there is at first a stand off....but Ally as Aliyana buckles up and introduces herself to him...There is a spark...a mental connection and talk about a piece. He is not forthcoming...he talks little and she senses his pain. He reveals the guilt he carries and how it is the basis for everything...This conversation takes a toll on both and is ended. She is left questioning what could have this beautiful, tattooed man so troubled... in so much pain...and create these works....<br><br>What she does not know is this artist is a new man carrying all the sins of the other man he once was...this man is Axel; ex con gang banger who is Austin's older brother...Levi's tarnished hero and tragic son of a mother he dearly loved...He is a man on his own personal cross for the sins he committed due to the needs of a family lost to alcoholism, poverty, spousal and child abuse and drug and gang violence. It took him being in prison to have a moment to see what transpired, the damage and then a fluke happenstance bringing him to the art world. His mentor has protected him... keeping his secret of who he actually is...but we, the readers, know and it is with this knowledge we see so much. <br><br>Axel comes to Austin's family 5 years sooner than expected...Austin loves his brother and wants him with him. Levi cannot forgive him for what he did to him personally or to Austin and his mother. Axel feeling this rejection from Levi makes himself scarce. He doesn't tell them what he has been doing... instead says he is working at the fish market all hours and not to worry.<br><br>The artist and the woman fall for each other hard. Every night they experience passion and a light shinning into his darkness. He reveals parts of himself to her and does not understand how this angel can be with this soiled man....so trusting. When they are together nothing else matters...it is only a matter of time when things will become complicated....and we know it.<br><br>This love story presents so many questions to consider...are we able to forgive the past...are we able to allow people to move forward and become better...is it encouraged...or is it human nature to think the worst because the worst is always what happened...And...most importantly... is there a driving force somewhere knowing that all steps had to happen to put into place actions which then cause the ultimate HEA....<br><br>As I mentioned in the beginning... I was with the tale every step even though there were times when I felt the resolution might have been a tad pat. There was also a lot of justification for past actions....But over all this was a story which held me in the palm of its hand. It had it all for me.... all the characters from the past books and the best Epilogue and bonus chapter. We were able to see the way things were down the line and it was very satisfying for Ally and Axel plus all the other characters...as it was the end of the series. <br><br>I highly recommend this series. It is emotional, insightful and not cookie cutter. Thank you Tillie Cole for giving me hours of thought provoking pleasure and heart squeezes. I will look for more from you. <br><br><b>~~~~ Before Reading ~~~~~</b><br>Jumping right in after staying up last night till the early morning reading Sweet Fall... so Ally, I am ready for you. <br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  </a>

<div id="review_934240660" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/934240660" />
    <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna"><img alt="✦❋Arianna✦❋" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420671997p2/23370948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/934240660?book_show_action=true">May 11, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✦❋Arianna✦❋" class="user" itemprop="url" name="✦❋Arianna✦❋" href="/user/show/23370948-arianna">✦❋Arianna✦❋</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer934240660" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4445224355180812338"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427804825i/14322780.jpg' width='400' height='402' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You are my hope, Ally. You’re every hope I’ve ever dared to have… la mia luce.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Ally, the female main character here is a 27 years old woman who works as a curator. She loves her job, so she’s more than exited she gets the opportunity to work with Elpidio, a talented, famous sculptor, one of the finest in the modern era. So she moves in Seattle for his showing. Allie is obsessed with Elpi’s work so when he meets him for the first time she’s more than intrigued by him. Elpi i</span>
  <span id="freeText4445224355180812338" style="display:none"><b>3.5 Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427804825i/14322780.jpg" width="400" height="402" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You are my hope, Ally. You’re every hope I’ve ever dared to have… la mia luce.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Ally, the female main character here is a 27 years old woman who works as a curator. She loves her job, so she’s more than exited she gets the opportunity to work with Elpidio, a talented, famous sculptor, one of the finest in the modern era. So she moves in Seattle for his showing. Allie is obsessed with Elpi’s work so when he meets him for the first time she’s more than intrigued by him. Elpi is tall, dark and handsome and he’s a broken man. He made a lots of mistakes in the past and now he’s trying to become a different man, making changes in his life. As the time passes and they start to know each other Elpi for the first time in his life lets someone in, Ally. Ally makes him feel like his life could get better and she gives him hope.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You should be running away from me, not willingly running into the darkness holding my fucking hand.”<br> 	“It’s too late,” she said quietly, “You’ve already consumed me. There is no turning back from you, not now. My hand’s never letting go of yours, eternal darkness or not.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I really wanted to love this one! I really did! Unfortunately I have more than one complain, so...It goes without saying this was not my fav book by this author or my fav book in the series. <br><br>I’m not gonna bore you with details about the plot, which btw, I found it very predictable. Overall the story was sweet, but a little too cheesy for my liking. What I really enjoyed the most was the writing which as always was fantastic and flawless. <br><br>Ally and Elpi were great characters. Ally is sweet and compassionate and I loved the fact she’s (too) judgemental. I loved Elpi more than Ally and I really felt for him. He’s a dark and tortured man and in my opinion he’s way more developed than Ally’s character. Despite his past, he’s a good man, a man who would do anything to protect his family. Another aspect of the story that I enjoyed was the connection and chemistry between the main characters. It was off the charts and very well done. They are great together and I really felt they are perfect for each other. <br><br>One thing that annoyed me like hell was the fact that everyone is crying for something. Too much crying for me!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1418145418ra/12686909.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427804825i/14322781.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nope, it's not!!*rolling eyes*<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1427804825ra/14322782.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was a very sad read and at times a little depressing for me. I think I need some pink fluffy unicorns dancing on rainbows….or not!<br>Unfortunately we have some miscommunication here, which of course created some unnecessary drama. Needless to say, I found all the drama to be OTT. (especially in the end)<br><br>Overall, this one was just an OK read for me!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4445224355180812338" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1134153702" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8880025909160043069"><b>5+++ “La mia luce” STARS<br/><br/><i>“Lightning,” I explained. “Together, we make…lightning…it’s the only way I can explain what feeling goes through me when I see you, talk to you…touch you…make love to you.”</i></b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/hRwahFZ' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445989080ra/16729726.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This is my FAVOURITE of this series and that's saying something as I LOVE this series. Wow!<br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/S4CxQN4' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450653256ra/17451639.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I'm a goner for anti-heroes, those dark brooding men that have done unthinkable things but there's still a sliver of hope for them. The oldest Carillo brother is just that!<br/><br/>Elipido (Axel Carillo) is <b>“dark, </b></span>
  <span id="freeText8880025909160043069" style="display:none"><b>5+++ “La mia luce” STARS<br><br><i>“Lightning,” I explained. “Together, we make…lightning…it’s the only way I can explain what feeling goes through me when I see you, talk to you…touch you…make love to you.”</i></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/hRwahFZ" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445989080ra/16729726.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is my FAVOURITE of this series and that's saying something as I LOVE this series. Wow!<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/S4CxQN4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450653256ra/17451639.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I'm a goner for anti-heroes, those dark brooding men that have done unthinkable things but there's still a sliver of hope for them. The oldest Carillo brother is just that!<br><br>Elipido (Axel Carillo) is <b>“dark, aggressively tattooed, and absolutely unconventionally beautiful.” </b><br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/elpi_zpsmjqokgyr.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450732950i/17461316._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo elpi_zpsmjqokgyr.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ally Prince (aka Aliyana Lucia) –<b>“I’d never seen anyone with eyes that bright, hair that dark, or a smile that fucking blinding.”</b><br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/Ally_zpsokbgmf6s.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450732950i/17461317._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo Ally_zpsokbgmf6s.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was beautifully moving! I felt this one deeply. The contrast of dark and light with Ally and Axe as well as the struggle and acceptance of the entire gang was heart wrenching and also beautiful. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/sweet%20hope_zpsbrv3rrpm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1450732950i/17461318._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo sweet hope_zpsbrv3rrpm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Lei era speranza…She was hope. La mia luce…my light.” <br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/tpuSVKS" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450653108ra/17451619.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>“She’d drilled through my fucking soul…the tainted soul I never ever wanted anyone to see.”</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/pFWOttw" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450653926ra/17451704.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And the epilogue ...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/m5bRVDB" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422917869ra/13563653.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I can't recommend this series enough!<br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/sweethope4_zpsudi1c3rk.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1261891365" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1261891365" />
    <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword"><img alt="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603584262p2/28146945.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1261891365?book_show_action=true">Apr 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword" href="/user/show/28146945-sara-ink-is-my-sword">Sara➽ Ink Is My Sword</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/25245349-sweet-hope">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1261891365" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13760205025953999055"><b>4.5 “Redemption” Stars</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>“He was living, breathing poetry. Not love poetry, but the poetry which tears out your heart, rips it to shreds, pushes it back into your chest, and makes you question what the hell just obliterated your soul?”</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Buddy-read with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30036082-warda' rel='nofollow noopener'>this lovely 3 hours ahead of me.</a><br/><br/>I will recommend you to read this book while listening to <b>Kiss The Rain by Yiruma</b>. Although I couldn’t think of this before, I am at least writing my review while listening to this. <br/><br/>My body is craving a re-read alrea</span>
  <span id="freeText13760205025953999055" style="display:none"><b>4.5 “Redemption” Stars</b><br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“He was living, breathing poetry. Not love poetry, but the poetry which tears out your heart, rips it to shreds, pushes it back into your chest, and makes you question what the hell just obliterated your soul?”</i>
</blockquote><br /><br />Buddy-read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/30036082-warda" rel="nofollow noopener">this lovely 3 hours ahead of me.</a><br /><br />I will recommend you to read this book while listening to <b>Kiss The Rain by Yiruma</b>. Although I couldn’t think of this before, I am at least writing my review while listening to this. <br /><br />My body is craving a re-read already, the feelings these books makes me feel are <b>my drug</b>. I honestly declare myself an addict.<br /><br />Was I expecting any less than a masterpiece from Tillie in this series? No. So why was I surprised I liked so much? I don’t know, she just has an awesome gift of giving me what I never thought I needed. It comes in the package of 200+ pages books with all the heart-wrenching scenes possible. And I really love her for that.<br /><br />Another gift Tillie has that needs to be called out is the ability to make you feel emotions since the prologue of her stories. I don’t know why that first pre-chapter always gets me. I know for sure that if someday I picked one fo her books, and the prologue doesn't make me feel stuff, I will probably not like it. <br /><br />I really don’t think I need to mention this again but just in case, it was addictive, I couldn’t stop. I literally kind of ditched Warda, ups. Also, <b>chapter 18</b> was my fav. <br /><br /><b>Plot:</b> <br /><br />This book follows the process of forgiveness and redemption of Elpidio a contemporary sculpture artist and Ally a woman who has never experienced that stoping-world-kinda-love <s>, to be honest, you are not alone in this one don’t worry</s>. The plot and progression were perfect, nothing felt rushed or out of place. The forgiveness wasn’t granted instantly and we got to see how our mc let his walls down, one by one. <br /><br /><b>Characters:</b><br /><br /><b>Elpidio:</b> I am not gonna tell you who he is, but you must get an idea by know. I was really worried I wasn’t gonna like him, or buy the redemption for this character. But I was so wrong, I am hitting myself for not giving Tillie more credit. His story is heartbreaking, and yes he is a sinner, but he also deserves forgiveness and the possibility of continuing on with his life and being loved. I was a huge fan of his long hair because it gave him a more hot and mysterious touch. The scenes of him when younger were one of my favorites. <br /><br /><b>Ally:</b> She was very much perfect, and I admire her passion for her work. I would have wanted a bit more of surprise or anger towards Elpidio revelation, to be honest. I am just so glad she got the love she was so desperately looking for. <br /><br />The rest of the characters are one we have already encountered on previous books, but then again I cannot finish this review without mentioning Levi. He is just very precious and lovely, I become a mama bear when he appears. <br /><br /><b>Relationship:</b><br />It was so heartbreaking and pure at the same time. It shows love can give us hope and can make us be better people. The chemistry was on point, and the sex scenes were so raw and intense, I am not kidding *flushes remembering*. I also loved how both of them would protect each other, they were honest about their feelings I loved it.<br /><br /><br /><b>If you love a very dark, redemption story. And you love art and good chemistry between the leads you need to try this book.</b> <br /><br /><i>“Darkness was consuming me. Darkness was taking my soul.”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13760205025953999055" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer845338622" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18132198224766244132"><b>5 Siempre Stars</b><br/><br/>From <i>Sweet Home</i> to <i>Sweet Hope</i>, no other author has owned their series like Tillie Cole. Each book builds up more of everything, never letting her readers down. It is no surprise that this last book was going to be epic!<br/><br/><a href='http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1427809243342_zpsxb1xlrq9.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427842399i/14327208.jpg' alt=' photo PhotoGrid_1427809243342_zpsxb1xlrq9.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>*PLEASE NOTE: YOU MUST READ SWEET FALL BEFORE THIS BOOK.*</b><br/><br/>This is the final story of Aliyana Lucia...Ally Prince as we all know and love her...<br/><br/><a href='http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1427809315303_zpsypm8g8am.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427842399i/14327209.jpg' alt=' photo PhotoGrid_1427809315303_zpsypm8g8am.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>All grown up and chasing her dreams as an art curator, she lives and breaths for her passions. Single and looking fo</span>
  <span id="freeText18132198224766244132" style="display:none"><b>5 Siempre Stars</b><br><br>From <i>Sweet Home</i> to <i>Sweet Hope</i>, no other author has owned their series like Tillie Cole. Each book builds up more of everything, never letting her readers down. It is no surprise that this last book was going to be epic!<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1427809243342_zpsxb1xlrq9.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427842399i/14327208.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1427809243342_zpsxb1xlrq9.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>*PLEASE NOTE: YOU MUST READ SWEET FALL BEFORE THIS BOOK.*</b><br><br>This is the final story of Aliyana Lucia...Ally Prince as we all know and love her...<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1427809315303_zpsypm8g8am.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427842399i/14327209.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1427809315303_zpsypm8g8am.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>All grown up and chasing her dreams as an art curator, she lives and breaths for her passions. Single and looking for that "lightning bolt" to go thru her. She wants a love as connecting as the feels she gets from one look at her favorite sculptures. She wants a deepness in her heart to settle over her like the works of the reclusive Elpidio.<br><br>Elpidio...<br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1427809339389_zpsdoyjsznz.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427842399i/14327210.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1427809339389_zpsdoyjsznz.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A man so broken...a past full of mistakes, a present full of guilt and pain, a future bleak. He seeks the light and wants nothing more than redemption. But how can anyone see more than his sins?<br><br>Match made in heaven...or hell. Two souls that belong, no crave to be together. Dark and light. Good and Bad. Hope and Despair. Ally and Elpi are beautiful together. I do not know another book couple whose story "broke" me so much. Tillie Cole made me feel. I felt the anger, I felt the loss, I was hurting, and I felt the rejection. I also was consumed in the passion, the want, the need and the acceptance. Her written words make me believe that love can be so deep...<b>"you are my awakening."</b><br><br><a href="http://s915.photobucket.com/user/KaBC1206/media/PhotoGrid_1427809285822_zpsoeem70bd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427842399i/14327211.jpg" alt=" photo PhotoGrid_1427809285822_zpsoeem70bd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>YES! This book is THAT GOOD! The writing was flawless. The story was angst and passion from the first written word. Tillie Cole can evoke feelings like no other, IMO. <br><br>So, Thank you for the whole Sweet Series, but mostly for this conclusion of all that was so perfectly executed. Thank you for making the characters of old supportive yet pivotal to the plot. Thank you for a deep love for the ages. Thank you for the sweet words of <i>Siempre</i>. Thank you for showing that the bonding of family, blood or not cannot be broken. Just, thank you for everything!</span>

<div id="review_762027070" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762027070" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762027070?book_show_action=true">Nov 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=2015">2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=i-want-it-now">i-want-it-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=explicit">explicit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=highly-emotional">highly-emotional</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-bad-boy">lead-character-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=dual-pov">dual-pov</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762027070" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8470439540113716377">FIVE+++ STARS<br/><br/><a href='http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/Teaser7_zpsiqwebnxw.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426840658i/14106906.jpg' alt=' photo Teaser7_zpsiqwebnxw.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>**NOTE: If you’re reading this review hoping to find out who Ally’s love interest is, you will NOT find that info here. Sorry, but this review will be spoiler free**</i><br/><br/><b>
  <i>Hope is a fervent, silent wish, that everything will turn out just as you dream… </i>
</b><br/><br/>Well folks, this is it. This is the end of the Sweet Home series and what a way to end it, too. This was just as emotionally packed as the previous books. Grab a box of tissues, guys, because this book will make your heart ache. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>T</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText8470439540113716377" style="display:none">FIVE+++ STARS<br><br><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/Teaser7_zpsiqwebnxw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426840658i/14106906.jpg" alt=" photo Teaser7_zpsiqwebnxw.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>**NOTE: If you’re reading this review hoping to find out who Ally’s love interest is, you will NOT find that info here. Sorry, but this review will be spoiler free**</i><br><br><b>
  <i>Hope is a fervent, silent wish, that everything will turn out just as you dream… </i>
</b><br><br>Well folks, this is it. This is the end of the Sweet Home series and what a way to end it, too. This was just as emotionally packed as the previous books. Grab a box of tissues, guys, because this book will make your heart ache. <br><br><b>
  <i>The most beautiful art is often born from the most desperate of circumstances.</i>
</b><br><br>Elpidio is finally getting his own exhibition. What he doesn’t understand is <i>why?</i> His mentor thinks he’s ready for his debut, but not Elpi. He doesn’t understand why anyone would want to pay any attention to him and his sculptures. Though they mean everything to him, his sculptures are reminder of his past; the meanings behind them private and haunting. He’s is a broken and talented man. He doesn’t want nor does he believe he deserves any of the attention until he meets Aliyana, the curator for his debut exhibition. For the first time in his life, he begins to <i>hope.</i><br><br><b>
  <i>She was fucking perfection. She was light. A blazing golden light…and when you’re locked in perpetual darkness, you’ll do anything to fucking chase that light.</i>
</b><br><br>Ally, known as Aliyana Garcia in the art world, is thrilled when she lands her dream assignment: Curating for Elpidio’s first show. Ally has loved this artist’s work ever since she saw one of his pieces up close. Though he’s a total recluse, he’s still her <i>absolute favorite modern artist.</i> The first time she sees him, she’s immediately struck at how dark and beautiful he is. She’s completely taken aback at how much he affects her. As for Elpi, he knows he doesn’t deserve a woman like Aliyana, but he can’t help but be attracted to her spirit and light. <br><br>Ally is desperate to know more about Elpi. Why is he so broken and angry? His vibe just screams for her to <i>stay away,</i> but the realization that she affects him just as much as he does her makes her want to stay. <br><br><b>
  <i>Fused.</i>
</b><br><br>I love Elpidio. He’s such a broken character and all I wanted was for him to be happy. I’m so happy fate chose Ally to be his light in darkness. The stars definitely aligned for these two. As for their chemistry…<b>HOT!!!</b> <br><br>Oh! And before anyone asks, the answer is, <i>YES</i>, you will get to see previous characters in this book. As a matter of fact, some of them truly melted my heart, made me swoon and made me cry. I might even be bold and say that couple characters stole my heart all over again. This was such a fantastic end to such an amazing series. I’m tearing up right now just thinking about it all, particularly the ending <i>*sniffles*</i>. <br><br>As I write these words, I can’t help but hope that we'll share the same experience reading this book. I say this because I went into this book knowing who Elpidio was, but yet the book still made a huge impact on me. I really don't know how Tillie does it. She never fails to write these amazing stories – ones that make me cry sad and happy tears. Bravo, Tillie! You’ve done it again. <br><br><i>THANK YOU, Tillie Cole, for giving me the honor of Beta reading this ❤</i><br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>♥♥♥ FOLLOW ME ♥♥♥</u>
</b><br><div>

<div id="review_1100547507" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1100547507" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1100547507?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=abused">abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=alpha-male-love">alpha-male-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=barely-made-it-through">barely-made-it-through</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=gangster">gangster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=healing">healing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-steam-alert">high-steam-alert</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=my-heart-can-barely-take-it">my-heart-can-barely-take-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=dark-and-gritty">dark-and-gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1100547507" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18022844582554611676"> <b>Solid 4.5 Teary eyed stars</b><br/><br/>Tillie Cole is the master of all things heartbreaking and beautiful. Sweet Hope is the final book in the Sweet Home Series and for me, it hit the mark! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428549181i/14444120._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Sweet Hope brings us home to the Alabama crew. The gang is all grown up. Ally is working as a curator and has been hired to put together a show for an upcoming sculptor. She is passionate about her work and passionate about the reclusive artist she will represent.<br/><br/> <b>“His work, it’s… it’s… it’s my soul. That’s the only wa</b></span>
  <span id="freeText18022844582554611676" style="display:none"> <b>Solid 4.5 Teary eyed stars</b><br><br>Tillie Cole is the master of all things heartbreaking and beautiful. Sweet Hope is the final book in the Sweet Home Series and for me, it hit the mark! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428549181i/14444120._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Sweet Hope brings us home to the Alabama crew. The gang is all grown up. Ally is working as a curator and has been hired to put together a show for an upcoming sculptor. She is passionate about her work and passionate about the reclusive artist she will represent.<br><br> <b>“His work, it’s… it’s… it’s my soul. That’s the only way I can explain it. It’s life, death, love, tragedy, and everything in between, every human condition… everything. His work speaks directly to my heart.”-Ally</b><br><br>To her delight the show she is going to put together is in Seattle. This means she can stay with her cousin Rome and Molly (sigh!) and also catch up with Austin and Lexi (double sigh)! She finds herself working late hours in order to properly showcase "the mysterious" Elpi's work to life. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428552694i/14444756.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Elpi looms in the shadows. He has many regrets in his life. He too is returning home. He doesn't get the same warm welcome that Ally receives. He has caused great pain and his family struggles with his return. He keeps his art a secret and leads them to believe that he is working at a local fish market.<br><br>Through the late nights in the gallery Ally works. Elpi lurks in the shadows watching her. He is drawn to her and captivated by the passion she shares for his work.<br><br> <b>"I saw in her eyes that she loved all this crap. And even crazier, she loved my work… the twisted, sculptures from my mind."-Elpi</b><br><br>Elpi doesn't feel like he is worth anything. He is so broken by the mistakes he is made. He doesn't feel like he deserves anything but pain. When Ally meets Elpi, he is like a wounded animal. He is terrified of the feelings she inspires and she is doesn't want to scare him away.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428549181i/14444121._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Their connection is deep. The art brings them closer together. They are very passionate people and together they create something deep and beautiful. <br><br><b>“I felt you. I felt you in its every curve. I felt like I was looking straight into your soul. I felt the love you poured into that sculpture… It made me reassess everything in my life… It made me want more… it’s difficult for me to explain.”-Ally</b><br><br>As their relationship grows stronger, Elpi struggles with revealing who he truly is. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[He is actually a well known character from the series. The nemesis to many evil things that have taken place over the years. When I realized this was his story, my heart burst. I was so grateful that Tillie Cole was giving resolution to Austin and Levi! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br> <b>"She was light. A blazing golden light. When you’re locked in perpetual darkness, you’ll do anything to chase that light. La mia luce…"-Elpi</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428552694i/14444757._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Ally evokes so much emotion from Elpi. She softens the hardness in his heart and opens the floodgates of his heart!<br><br><b>"I’d never once thought that I deserved a second chance, never wanted one. As far as I was concerned, I deserved to spend the rest of my life miserable for what I’d done. But here, deep inside the most beautiful woman I’d ever seen, the woman who just got me."-Elpi</b><br><br>When all is revealed, things are not easy for Elpi and Ally. They are determined to make a way together. Ally has to convince Elpi that he is more than worthy of love and happiness.<br><br> <b>“How the hell could I ever want anyone else now I’ve had you?”-Ally</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428552694i/14444758._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I truly enjoyed this book. There was a lot of crying and the emotions were high the entire read. However, I felt like they were 100% authentic. The combination of the hero's past and the fact that he is an artist validate the need for tears, blood shed, and the gnashing of teeth. If you are a fan of the Sweet Home Series, you absolutely MUST read this book. This book is full of emotion. There is a little bit of action but for the most part is a story rooted in pain and love. This story offers closure and reminds us that we are all worthy of love! Elpi and Ally's story was truly beautiful. <br><br> <b>“You are my hope , Ally. You’re every hope I’ve ever dared to have… la mia luce.”-Elpi</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1428552694ra/14444759.gif" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="18022844582554611676" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/103293496-bookadmirer?shelf=broken-hero">broken-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/103293496-bookadmirer?shelf=intense">intense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/103293496-bookadmirer?shelf=alpha-male-hero">alpha-male-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3178909050" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12341865418220917847">This is my most favorite book in this series. Axel is trying to redeem himself for the things he had done in the past. When I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___2__Carillo_Boys___1_' title='Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #2; Carillo Boys, #1) by Tillie Cole' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Fall</a> , I knew Axel wasn't a bad person. He grew up in poverty and the gang life saved him and his family from his alcoholic father afforded his mothers medicine and siblings expenses. <u>Everything he did was for his family. </u><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497554093ra/23036714.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>He wants to move on but also he is stuck because he thinks he doesn't deserve anything good. He is a damaged soul. He is living in the darkne</span>
  <span id="freeText12341865418220917847" style="display:none">This is my most favorite book in this series. Axel is trying to redeem himself for the things he had done in the past. When I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18759345.Sweet_Fall__Sweet_Home___2__Carillo_Boys___1_" title="Sweet Fall (Sweet Home, #2; Carillo Boys, #1) by Tillie Cole" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Fall</a> , I knew Axel wasn't a bad person. He grew up in poverty and the gang life saved him and his family from his alcoholic father afforded his mothers medicine and siblings expenses. <u>Everything he did was for his family. </u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1497554093ra/23036714.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He wants to move on but also he is stuck because he thinks he doesn't deserve anything good. He is a damaged soul. He is living in the darkness all his life, but then he met Ally, someone he feels connected to. Ally is his hope for life.<br><br>Ally is one of the best heroines I have read so far. She is <b>supportive, compassionate, and understanding.</b> She saw Axel's facade and understood him. She saw his worth when no one else's can and helped him to understand his worth as well. <br><br><blockquote>“You’re my reawakening.”</blockquote><br><br>And the romance between them was explosive. It was <b>sexy, hot, and intense.</b> It is one of the most <b>passionate romance</b> I have read ever. I don't know how to describe it. It was powerful and strong. It wasn't just lust but rather unconditional pure love. The sexual tension was just fantastic. Even the scenes were way too intense and they weren't even touching each other. And the sex scenes were just hot and very steamy. The undeniable heated passion between them was just beautiful. <b>Everything about them was intense, hot, and beautiful.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1590655066ra/29553648.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We also get to see the whole crew, Molly, Rome, Lexy, Austin, Cass, and Jimmy Don. Levi's anger was reasonable. He didn't know a lot of things. I loved how Austin always had axels back, even though he wasn't aware of the sacrifices Axel made for them, still, he was with him. When Ally revealed Axel's sacrifices to Levi and Austin, it was too emotional. And the ending was beautiful. When Levi, Austin, Axel, and their children sat at the roof and gazed at the stars. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1512378491ra/24595398.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a beautiful story of <b>moving forward, forgiveness, redemption, family, and love.</b> I loved how Axel redeemed himself and how Ally stood up for him. It was more than a worth read.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12341865418220917847" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NCx6wr7fSgpE90I0jRhPiLx+h3aJVgkbcvb8doRP3H8m7KvPr0depSlZ8EuUKcoVOjllMFVAV2XUTVq8BiPinw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer2064766663922598234">Amazon & USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses.</span>
  <span id="freeText2064766663922598234" style="display:none">Amazon &amp; USA Today Best Selling Author, Tillie Cole, is a Northern girl through and through. She originates from a place called Teesside on that little but awesomely sunny (okay I exaggerate) Isle called Great Britain. She was brought up surrounded by her English rose mother -- a farmer's daughter, her crazy Scottish father, a savagely sarcastic sister and a multitude of rescue animals and horses. <br />Being a scary blend of Scottish and English, Tillie embraces both cultures; her English heritage through her love of HP sauce and freshly made Yorkshire Puddings, and her Scottish which is mostly demonstrated by her frighteningly foul-mouthed episodes of pure rage and her much loved dirty jokes.<br /><br />Having been born and raised as a Teesside Smoggie, Tillie, at age nineteen, moved forty miles north to the 'Toon', Newcastle-Upon-Tyne, where she attended Newcastle University and graduated with a Bachelor of Arts honours degree in Religious Studies. She returned two years later to complete a Post-Graduate Certificate in Teaching High School Social Studies. Tillie, regards Newcastle to be a home from home and enjoyed the Newcastle Geordie way of life for seven 'proper mint' and 'lush' years.<br /><br />One summers day, after finishing reading her thousandth book on her much loved and treasured Kindle, Tillie turned to her husband and declared, "D'you know, I have a great idea for a story. I could write a book." Several months later, after repeating the same tired line at the close of another completed story, she was scolded by her husband to shut up talking about writing a novel and "just bloody do it!" For the first time in eleven years, Tillie actually took his advice (he is still trying to get over the shock) and immediately set off on a crazy journey, delving deep into her fertile imagination. <br /><br />Tillie, ever since, has written from the heart. She combines her passion for anything camp and glittery with her love of humour and dark brooding men (most often muscled and tattooed – they’re her weakness!). She also has a serious side (believe it or not!) and loves to immerse herself in the complex study of World Religions, History and Cultural Studies and creates fantasy stories that enable her to thread serious issues and topics into her writing -- yep, there's more to this girl than profanity and sparkles!<br /><br />After six years of teaching high school Social Studies and following her Professional Rugby Player husband around Europe, they have finally given up their nomadic way of life and settled in Calgary, Alberta where Tillie spends most of her days (and many a late night) lost in a writing euphoria or pursuing a dazzling career as a barrel-racing, tasselled-chap wearing, Stetson-sporting cowgirl... Ye-haw!<br /></span>

In her world of silence, Elsie has given up hope that her life will contain anything but constant struggle and pain… until the beautiful boy she has severely wronged comes to her rescue at precisely
